### Post by youngalfred on 2008-08-26
Hey im having some trouble with pdf previews.
When i installed my ubuntu, i immediately installed kde4-core to get kde, but now i have reverted back to gnome and removed kde.  now my pdf previews dont work. However, they do work when i sudo nautilus.  Has anyone encountered this before? if so how can it be fixed?  This is my evince-thumbnailers.schemas:

### Post by jedi-penguin on 2008-08-26
sounds like a permition problem. Try set the permition of the file to rw-rw-rw and see what happens

---

### Post by jedi-penguin on 2008-08-26
Oh and I believe there is a option in file manager that enable preview for certain type of files. Not harm to take a look

---

### Post by youngalfred on 2008-08-26
ok i think i have a theory.  it was only one pdf file that wasnt thumbnailing, i just didnt check my other ones.  After looking at another pdf file (it thumbnailed), i checked the properties of the pdf in question. it was made with microsoft word 2007.  my theroy is that word 07 doesnt save thumbnails in the files properly? and thats why it didnt show.

---
